href=\"https://www.beautyofbirds.com/attractingbirds.html\">Attracting Birds to your Garden</a></h2>\n<p class=\"rteindent1\">Who doesn't want to experience the colorful and fun creatures as close to home as possible? There is a lot you can do to invite them in.</p>\n<p><br></p>\n<hr><p><br></p>\n<h2>Bird Health</h2>\n<h3 style=\"padding-top:10px;\"><a href=\"diseases.htm\">Index of Bird Diseases / Health Problems and Research</a></h3>\n<h3 style=\"padding-top:10px;\"><a href=\"BirdSpeciesSyndroms.htm\">The Different Bird Species and Their Respective Syndromes</a></h3><h3>\n</h3><h3 style=\"padding-top:10px;\"><a href=\"birdnutrition.html\">Bird Nutrition</a> - the Key To Avian Health</h3><h3>\n</h3><h3 style=\"padding-top:10px;\"><a href=\"physicaltherapyinbirds.html\">Physical Therapy in Birds</a></h3>\n<h3 style=\"padding-top:10px;\"><a href=\"identifysickbirds.html\">Identifying a Potentially Sick Bird / Testing for Diseases &amp; Infections</a></h3><br><p class=\"rteindent1\">Learn more about: First Signs / Symptoms of a Sick Bird - Do-It-Yourself Disease / Sex Testing, Do-It-Yourself Bacterial Testing/ Microbiology, Lab &amp; Veterinary Resources ... New Bird &amp; Well Bird Exams </p>\n<h3 style=\"padding-top:10px;\"><a href=\"sickbirdcare.html\">Caring for a Sick Bird</a></h3>\n<h3 style=\"padding-top:10px;\"><a href=\"firstaid.html\">Bird Emergency Care / First Aid</a></h3>\n<p><br></p><hr><p><br></p>\n<h2>Birds - Our Wild Friends!</h2>\n<p>The stunning <strong>Central American</strong> <a href=\"https://www.beautyofbirds.com/purplethroatedmountaingems.html\">Purple-throated Mountain-gem</a> are second to none in terms of natural beauty.</p>\n<p><br></p>\n<p class=\"rteindent1\">They are one of the major tourist attractions in Costa Rica, where ecotourists come from afar to experience these delightful creatures in their natural habitat.</p>\n<p><br></p>\n<hr><p><br></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.beautyofbirds.com/crimsonsunbirds.html\"><img alt=\"Crimson Sunbirds\" src=\"images/birds/CrimsonSunbirdSM.jpg\" style=\"float:left; height:218px; width:166px\"></a></p>\n<p><br></p>\n<p>However, the stunning <strong><a href=\"https://www.beautyofbirds.com/crimsonsunbirds.html\">Crimson Sunbirds</a></strong> (and other sunbird species) from Asia have a lot in common with the American <a href=\"https://www.beautyofbirds.com/hummingbirds.htm\">hummingbirds</a>, such as small size, color plumages, and long skinny bills that are perfectly adapted for retrieving nectar from flower buds.</p>\n<p><br></p>\n<hr><p><br></p>\n<p><a class=\"Dusky Lory\" href=\"https://www.beautyofbirds.com/duskylory.html\" rel=\"Dusky Lory\"><img alt=\"Dusky Lories\" src=\"images/birds/DuskyLoriesSM.jpg\" style=\"float:right\"></a><a href=\"duskylory.html\"><strong>Dusky Lories</strong></a> aka Banded Lories or \"Duskies\" are unlike other parrots species.</p>\n<p>Their main diet consists of flowers, nectar and pollen. They are in demand in the pet market because of their striking beauty, but their loud natural vocalizations should be considered.</p>\n<p><br></p><hr><p><br></p>\n<p><img alt=\"The Mouth of a Chuckwillswidow (Bird)\" src=\"images/birds/ChuckwillswidowMouthSM.jpg\" style=\"float:right; height:198px; width:127px\">The North American <strong>Chuck-will's-widows</strong> are far from \"the usual.\" They have large, gaping mouths that allow them scoop up insects in flight.</p>\n<p><br></p>\n<p class=\"rteindent1\">These birds were named for their repetitive, loud, whistled \"chuck-will's-widow\" calls that are often heard at night.</p></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</section>\n</main>\n<div id=\"sidebar-second\" class=\"column sidebar\">\n<aside class=\"section\" role=\"complementary\">\n<div class=\"region region-sidebar-second\">\n<div id=\"block-ad\" class=\"block block-block-content block-block-content0fa419f4-54de-4a76-a9ba-4c92ac7f0f72\">\n<div class=\"content\">\n<div class=\"clearfix text-formatted field field--name-body field--type-text-with-summary field--label-hidden field__item\"><p><a href=\"http://www.ebay.com/itm/Avianweb-Arm-Hand-Perch-Patent-Pending-Made-in-the-USA-/282163951523\"><img alt=\"Bird Arm or Hand Perch\" data-entity-type=\"file\" data-entity-uuid=\"fee05b5a-625a-478a-ab88-d239e9c48aad\" src=\"/sites/default/files/inline-images/BoBArmPerchSM_0.jpg\"></a><a href=\"http://www.ebay.com/itm/Fred-Bird-Harness-and-6-Foot-Leash-The-Easiest-Safest-Harness-for-Pet-Birds-/272090975432\"><img alt=\"Bird Harness &amp;
